set routing-instances bbnlinband-ll protocols bgp group bbnlinband-ll import bbnlinband-ll_import
set routing-instances bbnlinband-ll protocols bgp group bbnlinband-ll export bbnlinband-ll_export
set routing-instances bbnlinband-ll protocols bgp group bbnlinband-ll peer-as 9829
set routing-instances bbnlinband-ll protocols bgp group bbnlinband-ll neighbor 172.20.128.194
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_import term END then reject
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_export term AGGREGATE from protocol aggregate
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_export term AGGREGATE then accept
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_export term direct from protocol direct
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_export term direct then accept
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_export term ACCESS from protocol access
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_export term ACCESS then accept
set policy-options policy-statement bbnlinband-ll_export term END then reject
set interfaces lo0 unit 20 description "bbnlinband-ll RI LOOPBACK"
set interfaces lo0 unit 20 family inet filter input vpn_protect_re
set interfaces ge-2/0/0 unit 3899 description " *** UPLINK-01 for routing-instance bbnlinband-ll *** ""
set interfaces ge-2/0/0 unit 3899 vlan-id 3899
set interfaces ge-2/0/0 unit 3899 family inet address 172.20.128.193/30

set routing-instances iptax instance-type virtual-router
set routing-instances iptax interface lo0.14
set routing-instances iptax routing-options autonomous-system 65027
set routing-instances iptax protocols bgp group iptax type external
set routing-instances iptax protocols bgp group iptax import iptax_import
set routing-instances iptax protocols bgp group iptax export iptax_export
set routing-instances iptax protocols bgp group iptax peer-as 9829
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_import term END then reject
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term DIRECT from protocol direct
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term DIRECT from route-filter 10.190.243.38/32 exact
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term DIRECT then accept
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term STATIC from protocol static
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term STATIC from route-filter 10.190.150.0/24 exact
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term STATIC from route-filter 10.190.156.0/24 exact
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term STATIC then accept
set policy-options policy-statement iptax_export term END then reject
set interfaces lo0 unit 14 description " iptax RI LOOPBACK "
set interfaces lo0 unit 14 family inet filter input iptax_protect_re
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term DENY_FIRST_FRAG from first-fragment
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term DENY_FIRST_FRAG then discard
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term DENY_NEXT_FRAG from is-fragment
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term DENY_NEXT_FRAG then discard
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_TCP_ESTABLISHED from protocol tcp
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_TCP_ESTABLISHED from tcp-established
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_TCP_ESTABLISHED then accept
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_BGP from protocol tcp
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_BGP from port bgp
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_BGP then accept
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_UDP_TRACEROUTE from protocol udp
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_UDP_TRACEROUTE from ttl 1
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_UDP_TRACEROUTE from destination-port 33434-33534
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_UDP_TRACEROUTE then policer udptrace_policer_5m
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_UDP_TRACEROUTE then accept
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_ICMP from protocol icmp
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_ICMP then policer icmp_policer_10m
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term PERMIT_ICMP then accept
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term DENY_LOG_OTHERS then count deny-others
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term DENY_LOG_OTHERS then log
set firewall family inet filter iptax_protect_re term DENY_LOG_OTHERS then discard
